  = only the MSS.  which we have cited and, at the most, not more than one minuscule
which we have not mentioned have supported the reading in question.
( ) as  , though there are one or more similar readings in other MSS.

Abbreviations:

al(ii) = other MSS.
pau(ci)= a few MSS. up to about a quarter of the known Minuscules.
compl(ures) = about a quarter to a half of the known Minuscules.
mu(lti) = about a half to three quarters of the known Minuscules.
pl(urimi) = over thre quarters of the known Minuscules.
